It's pre-computed (static) from the weights.\n    PER_CHANNEL = auto()\n    # The method uses one scaling factor per token. It's computed on-the-fly.\n    PER_TOKEN = auto()\n    # The method uses one scaling factor per group. It's pre-computed (static) from the weights.\n    PER_GROUP = auto()\n    # The KV cache is quantized in INT8.\n    INT8_KV_CACHE = auto()\n    # The KV cache is quantized in FP8.\n    FP8_KV_CACHE = auto()\n    # FP8 QDQ\n    FP8_QDQ = auto()\n    # FP8 rowwise\n    FP8_ROWWISE = auto()\n    # FP8 block scales for Deepseek\n    FP8_1x128_128x128 = auto()\n    # W4A8 qserve\n    W4A8_QSERVE = auto()\n    # FP4\n    NVFP4 = auto()\n    NVFP4_KV_CACHE = auto()\n    # W4A8 NVFP4\n    W4A8_NVFP4_FP8 = auto()\n    # W4A8 MXFP4\n    W4A8_MXFP4_FP8 = auto()\n    W4A8_MXFP4_MXFP8 = auto()\n    W4A16_MXFP4 = auto()\n\n    # The smallest power-of-two that is not used by a flag. You can restrict the test to the bits indicated by \"mask\".\n    def _all(self, bits, mask=VALID_FLAGS):\n        return (self & mask) == bits\n\n    # Is one of the bits of the mask set?\n    def _any(self, bits):\n        return (self & bits) != 0\n\n    def is_int8_weight_only(self):\n        return self._all(self.INT8_WEIGHTS, self.WEIGHTS_AND_ACTIVATIONS)\n\n    def mat1.sizes()[0], \"x\", mat1.sizes()[1], \" and \", mat2.sizes()[0], \"x\", mat2.sizes()[1], \")\");\n        m = mat1.sizes()[0];\n        n = mat2.sizes()[0];\n        k = mat2.sizes()[1] * 2;\n break;\n    case at::ScalarType::Float:\n        runGemm<float>(out, mat1, mat2, mat1Scale, mat2Scale, globalScale, m, n, k, b, config, fp4GemmType);\n        break;\n    default: 194→        \"out_dtype must be one of fp16/bf16/fp32. 231→    return fp4_bmm_impl(\n   232→        mat1, mat2, mat1Scale, mat2Scale, globalScale, static_cast<FP4GemmType>(fp4GemmType), out_dtype);\n   233→}\n   234→\n   235→class FP4GemmRunner : public
